    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',

        state: 'apple_oauth_state_59998974-e85e-4020-bb21-46b61d759a80'

<div id="descriptionContainer">
  
      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer6116584487277295304">Kevine Walcott's 'All of Me' is a holistic, boundless collection of poetry that puts life under a microscope and compels readers to examine every facet of their existence. From relationships and mother earth to intimacy, what it means to belong to a country and everything else in between, Walcott weaves together a beautiful tapestry of humanity.As a property professional b</span>
  <span id="freeText6116584487277295304" style="display:none">Kevine Walcott's 'All of Me' is a holistic, boundless collection of poetry that puts life under a microscope and compels readers to examine every facet of their existence. From relationships and mother earth to intimacy, what it means to belong to a country and everything else in between, Walcott weaves together a beautiful tapestry of humanity.As a property professional by trade, Kevine Walcott frequently comes in contact with the sheer breadth of humanity's cross-section. It's a series of collective experiences that have inspired her to turn to poetry, and capture her life, those she meets and the things that please and disgruntle her.In 'All of Me', Walcott's latest book, no subject's stone is left unturned in an attempt to capture the universe, its people and their emotions through a fascinating collection of verses.From the author of Institutionalised, a selection of nostalgic poems about nature, love, sex and patriotism."This is definitely a volume with something for everyone," explains the author. "No matter where you live, what your background is or what you're striving for in life, you'll find yourself within the pages. My goalwas to retain the unique hallmarks of poetry I've become known for, while allowing every reader to individualise the poems and extract true, vivid meaning."Continuing, "It's also a great volume for those who haven't yet spent much time exploring poetry, as the verses are so wide-ranging and can be adapted and defined according to anyone's unique personal situation. Pick up a copy - you'll be amazed at what you might find!"</span>
  <a data-text-id="6116584487277295304" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3088495152" />
    <a title="Ground Breaking" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/106915444-ground-breaking"><img alt="Ground Breaking" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1576584734p2/106915444.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3088495152?book_show_action=true">Dec 17, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ground Breaking" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ground Breaking" href="/user/show/106915444-ground-breaking">Ground Breaking</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/45687591-all-of-me">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3088495152" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6314677313119727275">Kevine Walcott's 'All of Me' will richly reward the attention of anyone who believes in self-expression to change lives - no enrich lives. So many paths of exploration defined in an anthology of the bravest insight and storytelling. Though poetry often has a fluid tone to each poem the words come through as a holistic meditation of society. microscope and compels readers to examine every facet of their existence. From relationships and mother earth to intimacy, what it means to belong to a count</span>
  <span id="freeText6314677313119727275" style="display:none">Kevine Walcott's 'All of Me' will richly reward the attention of anyone who believes in self-expression to change lives - no enrich lives. So many paths of exploration defined in an anthology of the bravest insight and storytelling. Though poetry often has a fluid tone to each poem the words come through as a holistic meditation of society. microscope and compels readers to examine every facet of their existence. From relationships and mother earth to intimacy, what it means to belong to a country and everything else in between, "Walcott weaves together a beautiful tapestry of humanity.As a property professional by trade, Kevine Walcott frequently comes in contact with the sheer breadth of humanity's cross-section." I think is the best sentence in the description of the book.<br /><br />As a poet myself, I am inspired by the movement of poets who speak out in a tone that can be heard. Not loud or branding oneself, not someone with agendas and hate. I respect authors who achieve their God given talent with a collective of memories and experiences that can transcend generations. The best poetry through the decades, has been cultural influence and social movement through Spoken Word.<br /><br />Kevine Walcott is a dedicated member of the poetic society, in my opinion. Good luck.<br /></span>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3054591087" />
    <a title="Re:Views" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/105627157-re-views"><img alt="Re:Views" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1574169727p2/105627157.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3054591087?book_show_action=true">Nov 19, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Re:Views" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Re:Views" href="/user/show/105627157-re-views">Re:Views</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3054591087" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3713287276244861310">I'm not a big reader of poetry, so when I do read it, I like it to really make an impact and not to be to stuffy and needlessly wordy. 'All of Me' by Kevine Walcott an anthology full of poems that are accessible and meaningful, with something that will resonate with everyone. The poetry explores so many different themes, from love and lust, and from mental illness to the Mona Lisa.<br/><br/>I think he one that stuck with me the most was 'The Nation-State' as it is so current and so insightful, and I think</span>
  <span id="freeText3713287276244861310" style="display:none">I'm not a big reader of poetry, so when I do read it, I like it to really make an impact and not to be to stuffy and needlessly wordy. 'All of Me' by Kevine Walcott an anthology full of poems that are accessible and meaningful, with something that will resonate with everyone. The poetry explores so many different themes, from love and lust, and from mental illness to the Mona Lisa.<br /><br />I think he one that stuck with me the most was 'The Nation-State' as it is so current and so insightful, and I think there could be many different interpretations of it depending on your views.<br /><br />“As you permeate every sphere of our lives, roll back the State and power to the people, they cry –<br />But could anyone live without your ‘big brother’ eyes?<br />With your army, the police on the beat, and the cameras on our streets, you make us safe”<br /><br />It is an anthology of such different poems, each of which will make you think and feel in different ways.<br /><br /></span>

          </span>

<div id="review_3083536590" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3083536590" />
    <a title="Red Apple" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/106748550-red-apple"><img alt="Red Apple" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1576251870p2/106748550.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3083536590?book_show_action=true">Dec 13, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Red Apple" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Red Apple" href="/user/show/106748550-red-apple">Red Apple</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3083536590" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15654812879248166494">All of Me by Kevine Walcott is a collection of poetry and I found it so refreshing to read. Walcott reminds everyone of some of the beauty that still exists in the world, which is worth noting in these negative times we live in. Anyone who is looking for some great poetry with a direct but positive and uplifting message to read then this book is definitely for you. This is some great poetry and I’m glad I picked it. All of Me took me on a journey of so many different, meaningful themes. Well don</span>
  <span id="freeText15654812879248166494" style="display:none">All of Me by Kevine Walcott is a collection of poetry and I found it so refreshing to read. Walcott reminds everyone of some of the beauty that still exists in the world, which is worth noting in these negative times we live in. Anyone who is looking for some great poetry with a direct but positive and uplifting message to read then this book is definitely for you. This is some great poetry and I’m glad I picked it. All of Me took me on a journey of so many different, meaningful themes. Well done Kevine, this is a great book.</span>
  <a data-text-id="15654812879248166494" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3064735630?book_show_action=true">Nov 27, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3064735630" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9317968889019050006">Kevine Walcott's 'All of Me' will richly reward the attention of anyone who believes in self-expression to change lives - no enrich lives. So many paths of exploration defined in an anthology of the bravest insight and storytelling. Though poetry often has a fluid tone to each poem the words come through as a holistic meditation of society. microscope and compels readers to examine every facet of their existence. From relationships and mother earth to intimacy, what it means to belong to a count</span>
  <span id="freeText9317968889019050006" style="display:none">Kevine Walcott's 'All of Me' will richly reward the attention of anyone who believes in self-expression to change lives - no enrich lives. So many paths of exploration defined in an anthology of the bravest insight and storytelling. Though poetry often has a fluid tone to each poem the words come through as a holistic meditation of society. microscope and compels readers to examine every facet of their existence. From relationships and mother earth to intimacy, what it means to belong to a country and everything else in between, "Walcott weaves together a beautiful tapestry of humanity.As a property professional by trade, Kevine Walcott frequently comes in contact with the sheer breadth of humanity's cross-section." I think is the best sentence in the description of the book. <br /><br />As a poet myself, I am inspired by the movement of poets who speak out in a tone that can be heard. Not loud or branding oneself, not someone with agendas and hate. I respect authors who achieve their God given talent with a collective of memories and experiences that can transcend generations. The best poetry through the decades, has been cultural influence and social movement through Spoken Word. <br /><br />Kevine Walcott is a dedicated member of the poetic society, in my opinion. Good luck. </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3061065935" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer250174072536400944">Kevine Walcott’s collection of poetry, All of Me, is an outstanding anthology that really demonstrates the staying power and relevance of poetry in the modern-day. <br/><br/>Walcott leaves no stone unturned as he tackles a wide array of different subjects, including things like love, loss, and even mental illness. Walcott does not shy away from any of these topics and as such, they feel all the more human and significant. It is hard to deny the impact that these poems have on the reader. His riffs on mode</span>
  <span id="freeText250174072536400944" style="display:none">Kevine Walcott’s collection of poetry, All of Me, is an outstanding anthology that really demonstrates the staying power and relevance of poetry in the modern-day. <br /><br />Walcott leaves no stone unturned as he tackles a wide array of different subjects, including things like love, loss, and even mental illness. Walcott does not shy away from any of these topics and as such, they feel all the more human and significant. It is hard to deny the impact that these poems have on the reader. His riffs on modern life are both refreshing and thought-provoking. <br /><br />In an age where we all live behind screens and have less and less meaningful interactions, All of Me is an excellent reminder of some of the beauty that exists in the world. This is the perfect book to read for those who are looking for some excellent contemporary poetry. <br /></span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('VpeGMgddRxwCDsNfjilgyuMeUq1rDoZavpzQnUmPM0guTQrCIFw0NZLfGWR+tESvPxdkY143ZLgtNBmGGgoANA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('3w/Ksfd3Vh7mio06mY0GAUgvDdHXZp6WfncvKOm2yoSn1UZB0HYlN3ZbVwFpECJklCY7H+JffHTt3+YzujP5+A==')})
  }

They find art, of course, and a world of beautiful landscapes, warm temperatures, and, yes, wonderful food. But they also find a ghost of their past, and it’s not Vincent Van Gogh but a woman Ben once loved and a man, Zach, a well-known jazz musician, who teach them some hard lessons about art and life, as well as the art of life.  A SUMMER OF GOOD-BYES resonates with the warmth of France’s southern sun, famous artists, and violent conflicts. It’s a vital, romantic story filled with the tensions of love and marriage, sexual longing and family loyalty, and the struggle to live in the face of impending death and loss.<\/span>\n  <a
